class=\"day\">21</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>We love any opportunity to take a virtual escape on a Royal Caribbean cruise, and that is why every Friday we share our readers' favorite Royal Caribbean cruise photos. &nbsp;It is a showcase of cruising fun, and you are invited!</p>\n<p>Without further ado, we present this week's edition of Friday Photos. Enjoy!</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/20170330_112626.jpg?1000\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img docked in Costa Maya, taken by Ken in March 2017.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_2067.jpg?579\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_2067.jpg?579\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 375px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Next is a photo of Columbus Cove in Labadee, taken by Tommy Koth.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_0961.jpg?443\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_0961.jpg?443\" style=\"width: 300px; height: 400px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Stephanie Anderson sent in this photo of the brand new floating bar in Labadee. &nbsp;</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_6694.JPG?72\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_6694.JPG?72\" style=\"width: 300px; height: 400px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Cristina Myers sent this photo of Sarah looking over the Royal Promenade on Liberty of the Seas.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_0740.jpg?715\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_0740.jpg?715\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 375px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Irina shared this photo from Navigator of the Seas, taken in March 2017.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_2063.jpg?692\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/IMG_2063.jpg?692\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 375px;\"></a></p>\n<p>Bill Bartman took this photo from his cabana on CocoCay, with a perfect view of Anthem of the Seas.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/Madalynn.jpg?30\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/friday-photos/Madalynn.jpg?30\" style=\"width: 300px; height: 400px;\"></a></p>\n<p>We round out this week's edition of Friday Photos with this photo of Jimmy Burns' 4-year-old daughter, Madalynn, excited to watch the ocean on her first cruise.</p>\n<p>Thank you to everyone who shared their photos this week, and we invite everyone to send in href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/21/royal-caribbean-first-quarter-2017-earnings-call-scheduled\">Royal Caribbean First Quarter 2017 Earnings Call Scheduled</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/financial-news\">Financial News</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">21</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Royal Caribbean will hold a conference call on April 28, 2017&nbsp;at 10am to discuss its first quarter 2017&nbsp;financial results.</p>\n<p>The call will be available on-line at the company's investor relations web site, <a href=\"http://www.rclinvestor.com\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">www.rclinvestor.com</a>. To listen to the call by phone, please dial (877) 663-9606 in the US and Canada. International phone calls should be made to (706) 758-4628. There is no passcode or meeting number. A replay of the webcast will be available at the same site for a month following the call.</p>\n</div><div class=\"addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style \" class=\"node\"><h2 class=\"title\"><a href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/20/royal-caribbean-ceo-talks-new-ships-innovations-and-options-coming-soon-the-cruise-line\">Royal Caribbean CEO talks new ships, innovations and options coming soon to the cruise line</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/michael-bayley\">Michael Bayley</a></li><li><a href=\"category/category/cococay\">CocoCay</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">20</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Royal Caribbean CEO Michael Bayley <a href=\"http://www.travelweekly.co.uk/articles/277322/big-interview-michael-bayley-president-and-chief-executive-of-royal-caribbean-international\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">spoke with Travel Weekly</a> about a variety of topics this week, which confirmed or announced a number of changes coming to the cruise line in the next few years.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/michael-bayley-harmony.jpg?itok=4LuIDfFV\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 333px;\"></p>\n<p>Among the topics mentioned were</p>\n<ul>\n<li><strong>Quantum 4</strong> (also known as Quantum Plus), will set sail in 2019 and spend its first winter in China, and, if it is not deployed to the UK earlier that summer, will spend the whole summer in China too.</li>\n<li><strong>Symphony of the Seas</strong> will feature, \"an experience for kids and the kid in you, something for adventure seekers but in a nice, safe way.\"</li>\n<li>Royal Caribbean is working on several product enhancements on <strong>Symphony of the Seas</strong> to improve the dining, entertainment and service.&nbsp;All will start to be <strong>revealed next month</strong>.</li>\n<li>Bayley indicated <strong>Majesty of the Seas could be sailing to Cuba too</strong>, \"We have 40-50 sailings calling into Havana in 2017, starting in April  mostly on Empress of the Seas but also a few on Majesty of the Seas.\"</li>\n<li>Royal Caribbean will build a \"massive water park\" in CocoCay that, \"will eclipse any other water park in the world.\"</li>\n<li>Guests on CocoCay may be able to <strong>get off the ship and stay there overnight</strong>, \"we will be adding some private cabana accommodation for Suite Class guests who may want to get off and stay for a few days in total luxury and privacy before hopping on another ship to come home.\"</li>\n</ul>\n<p>You can <a href=\"http://www.travelweekly.co.uk/articles/277322/big-interview-michael-bayley-president-and-chief-executive-of-royal-caribbean-international\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">read the entire interview with Michael Bayley on TravelWeekly</a>.</p>\n</div><div class=\"addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style \" Comments</a></div></div><div class=\"node\"><h2 class=\"title\"><a href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/19/royal-caribbeans-first-cruise-cuba-sets-sail\">Royal Caribbean's first cruise to Cuba sets sail</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/cuba\">Cuba</a></li><li><a href=\"category/category/empress-of-the-seas\">Empress of the Seas</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">19</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Royal Caribbean's Empress of the Seas set sail today from Miami, Florida marking the beginning of an historical voyage that will mark Royal Caribbean International's first visit to Cuba.</p>\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-1\" data-tweet-id=\"854789710635552770\" style=\"position: static; the Seas to the tune of live music, Cuban coffee and Cuba Libres served to guests as they boarded.</p>\n<p>Empress of the Seas is on a 5-night inaugural sailing to Cuba, which will make the historic visit to Havana, Cuba on Sunday, April 23, 2017.</p>\n<p>As guests boarded Empress of the Seas, Royal Caribbean had special Cuba photo opportunities set up, along with plenty of fanfare.</p>\n<twitterwidget class=\"twitter-tweet twitter-tweet-rendered\" id=\"twitter-widget-2\" data-tweet-id=\"854711576636436480\" style=\"position: static; visibility: visible; display: block; class=\"issuuembed\"></div>\n<script type=\"text/javascript\" src=\"//e.issuu.com/embed.js\" async=\"true\"></script><p>Royal Caribbean brought Empress of the Seas back into its fleet in early 2016, specifically because its size was a perfect fit for Havana harbor.</p>\n</div><div class=\"addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style \" class=\"node\"><h2 class=\"title\"><a href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/19/5-things-love-about-royal-caribbeans-liberty-of-the-seas\">5 things to love about Royal Caribbean's Liberty of the Seas</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/liberty-seas\">Liberty of the Seas</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">19</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Liberty of the Seas is one of three Freedom Class cruise ships in Royal Caribbean's fleet, and offers some incredible amenities and activities onboard. Here are five really fun things to enjoy while aboard Liberty of the Seas.</p>\n<h2>5. Sabor</h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/IMG_4580_0.JPG?itok=UCFX4ugF\" style=\"width: 500px; height: 333px;\"></p>\n<p>What can we say, we&nbsp;<em>really&nbsp;</em>like Sabor Modern Mexican on Royal Caribbean's shjps and if you happen to go on a Liberty of the Seas cruise, a visit to this specialty restaurant is a must do.</p>\n<p>Sabor distinguishes itself by offering excellent quality Mexican food. &nbsp;This is not a run-of-the-mill forgetful Mexican food. Rather, you get creative dishes made from fresh ingredients.</p>\n<p>By far, the freshly made guacaomole is the star of Sabor. Sure, we cannot get enough ahi tuna tacos,&nbsp;Chicken-Stuffed Jalapeos or those wonderful margaritas, but the guacamole is just so good that it alone is worth the visit.</p>\n<h2>4. Splashaway Bay Aqua Park</h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/IMG_2377.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"333\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/IMG_2377.jpg?itok=6xLJkvl1\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>Liberty of the Seas is one of the few Royal Caribbean ships to offer its guests the cruise line's newest take on aquatic adventure park. &nbsp;In fact, Liberty of the Seas was the first ship in the fleet to recieve Splashaway Bay.</p>\n<p>So what makes Splashaway Bay so cool? This fun spot is full of waterlides, water cannons, waterfalls and more. &nbsp;It is the kind of place kids will never want to leave. The&nbsp;gigantic drench bucket and a multi-platform jungle-gym mean not only will the kids get (and stay) drenched while playing there, they are going to have a great time doing it.</p>\n<p>What makes Splashaway Bay special is the fact it is the latest and greatest water play area option in Royal Caribbean's fleet. &nbsp;Including some of the fun things to do included later on in this blog post, it makes Liberty of the Seas one of the best ships if you are cruising with kids.</p>\n<h2>3. Panoramic staterooms</h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/liberty-pano-room.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"333\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/liberty-pano-room.jpg?itok=1b55r3H-\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>If you think staterooms on a cruise ship are the same from ship to ship, then you need to see the panoramic oceanview staterooms on Liberty of the Seas.</p>\n<p>A few years ago Royal Caribbean began adding staterooms that have floor-to-ceiling glass windows that provide a spectacular view. &nbsp;Granted, these rooms lack a balcony, but having such an unobstructed view at your disposal is such a treat.</p>\n<p>Ranging in size from 191 to 215 square feet, the panoramic oceanview staterooms on Liberty of the Seas offer lots of space and a view you never tire of seeing.</p>\n<h2>2. Saturday Night Fever</h2>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/saturday-night-fever.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"375\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/saturday-night-fever.jpg?itok=7gw5v-9-\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>Select Royal Caribbean ships offer <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2015/10/20/broadway-shows-royal-caribbean-everything-you-need-know\">Broadway shows</a> for their guests to enjoy, including Liberty of the Seas. Since 2011, Liberty of the Seas has been offering guests the opportunity to see Saturday Night Fever onboard, and the show is included with their cruise fare.</p>\n<p>The musical depicts Tony, an ambitious Brooklyn teen who spends his Saturday nights disco dancing. It is a nostalgic look back to the 1970s with plenty of classic music to enjoy.</p>\n<h2>1. Waterslides</h2>\n<p></p>\n<a class=\"photosTop\" name=\"photosTop0\"></a><div class=\"view view-ship-section-gallery view-id-ship_section_gallery view-display-id-default view-dom-id-17e24b70703e0ad7239fa53ca3ad7644\">\n<div class=\"view-content\">\n<div class=\"views-nivo-slider-view slider-wrapper theme-default nivo-control-thumbs\">\n<div id=\"views-nivo-slider-ship-section-gallery-default\" class=\"views-nivo-slider clearfix nivo-slider-processed nivoSlider\" style=\"width: 610px; height: 458px;\">\n              <img data-thumb=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/nivo_thumb/public/galleries/pool-area-and-sports-deck/IMG_1165.JPG?itok=5Nilka9b\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" Steve Ritter.</p>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p>No sailing aboard Liberty of the Seas is complete without a few rides down its amazing \"Perfect Storm\" waterslides.&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Liberty of the Seas features the first Boomerang style waterslide at sea, named&nbsp;Tidal Wave. &nbsp;The hair-raising slide features a steep drop that propels riders up a near vertical wall for a moment of weightlessness and into free fall.</p>\n<p></p>\n<a class=\"photosTop\" name=\"photosTop2\"></a><div class=\"view view-ship-section-gallery excursion.</p>\n<p><strong>What is this about?</strong></p>\n<p><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/podcast/episode-194-private-journeys-shore-excursion\"><img alt=\"\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/podcastlogo2.jpg\" style=\"margin: 10px; float: right; width: 240px; height: 240px;\"></a>In this episode, Matt and Christie discuss Royal Caribbean's relatively new option for guests that want a completely customizable shore excursion with all the benefits of booking through Royal Caribbean.</p>\n<p>It feels like there are certain ports where either no existing excursions stand out as perfect choices, or there is too much compromise with what is available. &nbsp;Enter, Private Journeys, which allows guests to work with Royal Caribbean to come up with the perfect private tour just for them.</p>\n<p>We talk about who Private Journeys is a good fit for, share our recent experiences trying it out and review the experience from start to finish.</p>\n<p><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/podcast/episode-194-private-journeys-shore-excursion\">Listen right now</a>, or subscribe via <a class=\"node\"><h2 class=\"title\"><a href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/19/spotted-royal-caribbean-unlimited-alcohol-and-internet-combo-package\">Spotted: Royal Caribbean unlimited alcohol and internet combo package</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/drink-packages\">Drink Packages</a></li><li><a href=\"category/category/voom\">Voom</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">19</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Royal Caribbean guests in the market for an unlimited alcohol package and internet access will want to take notice of a new option Royal Caribbean has added.</p>\n<p>The <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2016/10/20/depth-look-royal-caribbeans-deluxe-drink-package\">Deluxe Drink Package</a>&nbsp;and <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/02/07/guide-royal-caribbean-voom-wifi-internet-prices-and-tips\">Voom</a> One Device offers guests the deluxe beverage unlimited alcohol package and a one-device Voom plan in one combo.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/sip-stream-after-min.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"329\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/sip-stream-after-min.jpg?itok=GkdA7xKU\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>The cost of this package is listed at $54&nbsp;per guest, per day. Compared to buying the two options separately, there are potential savings to the guest.</p>\n<p>Here is an example for what each would individually cost for a 7-night cruise on Harmony of the Seas.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/sip-steam-before-min.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"509\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/sip-steam-before-min.jpg?itok=EO-qskX9\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>This \"Sip and Stream\" combo package has appeared in the past but has also disappeared quite quickly. &nbsp;If you are interested in it, our advice is to book it immediately. &nbsp;Keep in mind that <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2016/10/29/how-cancel-and-rebook-pre-cruise-purchases-royal-caribbeans-cruise-planner\">Cruise Planner purchases are able to be canceled</a> prior to the start of the cruise.</p>\n</div><div class=\"addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style \" Comments</a></div></div><div class=\"node\"><h2 class=\"title\"><a href=\"https://www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2017/04/18/spotted-royal-caribbean-adds-new-swim-bar-labadee\">Spotted: Royal Caribbean adds new swim-up bar in Labadee</a></h2><span class=\"terms-label\">In: </span><div class=\"tags\"><div class=\"item-list\"><ul><li><a href=\"category/category/labadee\">Labadee</a></li></ul></div></div><div class=\"date\"><span class=\"day\">18</span><span class=\"month\">Apr</span><span class=\"year\">2017</span></div><div class=\"content\"><p>Royal Caribbean has opened up a new floating bar for guests to enjoy at its private destination in Haiti, known as Labadee.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-2.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"375\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-2.jpg?itok=irpUPOSC\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>The new floating bar is located at Adrenaline Beach, and is surrounded by water. Guests simply walk through the ocean to the bar, climb up and order and enjoy a drink. Royal Caribbean Blog reader&nbsp;Sebastian Sderstrm shared these photos, from his recent cruise stop on Independence of the Seas.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-1.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"375\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-1.jpg?itok=VCbE_MAk\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-3.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"375\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-3.jpg?itok=pA1DmGQf\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-4.jpg\" rel=\"lightbox\" class=\"lightbox-processed\"><img alt=\"\" class=\"image-500px\" height=\"375\" src=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/sites/default/files/styles/500px/public/blog-images/labadee-floating-bar-4.jpg?itok=G7DRvyE6\" width=\"500\"></a></p>\n<p>The floating bar is located underneath the <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2015/07/02/excursion-focus-zipline-labadee\">zip line</a>, which should provide for some fun views as guests enjoy a beverage at the bar.</p>\n<p>Royal Caribbean <a href=\"//www.royalcaribbeanblog.com/2016/08/02/spotted-new-swim-bar-royal-caribbeans-private-island-coco-cay\">added a floating bar</a> to its other private destination, CocoCay in the Bahamas, last summer and has become quite popular with guests.</p>\n<p><strong>Do you want to try this bar on your next cruise stop in Labadee? Tell us your thoughts in the comments!</strong></p>\n</div><div class=\"addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style \"
